Designing it with single player accessibility and multiplayer gameplay would have been a better approach This is the only game since Demons Souls (2009) that I felt no active desire to buy and that will remain until the there is an adjustment for Single Player Rogue like modes like God of War Ragnarok Valhalla, The Last of Us Part II No Escape, Bloodborne's Chalice Dungeons and Resident Evil 4/Village's Mercenaries are excellent ways to keep players engaged with the combat system without having to replay the main game. Elden Ring had no such mode, to be fair neither did any of the other titles (except Bloodborne) Introducing old assets as a way to re-engage players with an improved engine is an excellent idea, but making it accessible to multiplayer only to this extent seems to ignore players who DONT have access to friends with intimate knowledge and experience playing Elden Ring, and narrowing the sales to those exclusively in communities and not to those who wish to engage with the new system on their own.
